Introduction

Base URL: http://127.0.0.1:8000

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Activity

GET api/activity/list

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/list"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/list"
);

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 60
x-ratelimit-remaining: 50
access-control-allow-origin: *
 

{
    "activities": [
        {
            "id": 2,
            "title": "Etkinlik 2",
            "description": "<p> Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipiscing elit,sed do eiusmod tempor incididunt ut labore et dolore magna aliqua.</p>",
            "image": "http://127.0.0.1:8001/storage/activity_images/9EShJVkDl8i73zdODQNmwpOmFaYfk5AK1jQacPT9.jpg",
            "start_time": "11.03.2002 16:03",
            "end_time": "21.11.1989 04:43"
        }
    ]
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

GET api/activity/list

POST api/activity/get

  • Etkinliklerin gönderilen id ye göre verisini döndürür.
  • Ekinlikteki personel sayısını, detaylarını
  • Sponsor sayısını ve detaylarını döndürür
  • Göndermeniz Gereken Tek Veri activity_id
Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/get" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"activity_id\": 17
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/get"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "activity_id": 17
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/activity/get

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

activity_id   integer   

Example: 17

POST api/activity/join

  • Göndermeniz Gereken Veriler activity_id, phone, password
Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/join"

    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/activity/join"

Authentication

POST api/auth/login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/auth/login" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"phone\": \"consequuntur\",
    \"password\": \"5\\\"p5\\\"z:%%?mc@]Ym*m\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/auth/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Accept": "application/json",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "phone": "consequuntur",
    "password": "5\"p5\"z:%%?mc@]Ym*m"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/auth/login

Headers

Accept      

Example: application/json

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

phone   string   

The phone number of the user. Example: consequuntur

password   string   

The password of the user. Example: 5"p5"z:%%?mc@]Ym*m

POST api/auth/register

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/auth/register" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"dolorem\",
    \"phone\": \"saepe\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/auth/register"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "dolorem",
    "phone": "saepe"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/auth/register

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

name   string   

The phone number of the user. Example: dolorem

phone   string   

The password of the user. Example: saepe

GET api/city/list

POST api/city/get

City id gönderilen şehrin bilgilerini ve ilçe verisini döndürür.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/city/get" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"city_id\": 13
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/city/get"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "city_id": 13
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Status Codes

  • 200 Başarılı
  • 422 Validator Hatası
  • 401 Unauthorized Hatası

Bu müşteri bilgilerini döndürecek

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/get" \
    --header "Bearer: {token}"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/get"
);

const headers = {
    "Bearer": "{token}",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

Customer (Update)

POST api/customer/update/profile

Bu müşterinin profil bilgilerini güncelleyecek endpoint

  • city_id ve district_id zorunlu alan değildir istenirse gönderilebilir
  • Tarih formatı 2001-09-08 şeklinde (YY-AA-GG) şeklinde olmaıdır
Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/update/profile" \
    --header "Bearer: {token}"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/update/profile"
);

    "Bearer": "{token}",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,

POST api/customer/update/password

Bu müşterinin şifre bilgilerini güncelleyecek endpoint
Gerekli alanlar

  • password
  • password_confirmation
Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/update/password" \
    --header "Bearer: {token}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"password\": \")\\\"-H<UEv.N@b*\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/customer/update/password"
);

const headers = {
    "Bearer": "{token}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "password": ")\"-H<UEv.N@b*"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.

GET api/salons/list

Search

POST api/search/service

Burada hizmet türüne veya şehir verisine göre işletmelerin verisi döndürülür. Not: city_id ve service_id ikisinden sadece biri de gönderilebilir.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/service?service_id=consectetur&city_id=nisi"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/service"
);

const params = {
    "service_id": "consectetur",
    "city_id": "nisi",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/search/service

Query Parameters

service_id   string  optional  

Example: consectetur

city_id   string  optional  

Example: nisi

POST api/search/business/type

Burada işletme türüne veya şehir verisine göre işletmelerin verisi döndürülür. Not: city_id ve category_id ikisinden sadece "biri de" gönderilebilir.

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/business/type?category_id=sapiente&city_id=sed"
const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/business/type"
);

const params = {
    "category_id": "sapiente",
    "city_id": "sed",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/search/business/type

Query Parameters

category_id   string  optional  

Example: sapiente

city_id   string  optional  

Example: sed

POST api/search/business/name

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/business/name" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"voluptas\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://127.0.0.1:8000/api/search/business/name"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "voluptas"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.
